<br />
This is a gentler version of Ebene Fume, and a more rounded version of Eilish no. 2. Having said that, it does not perform as well as either of those on my skin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="2099124"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=2099124#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2068305" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-20">01/20/24 02:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Interesting scent. It really does give the feeling of the color brown like the bottle and ingredients. I bought this blind because I found the idea of a desert landscape in tandem whiskey and cacao a lofty and compelling idea, and I wanted to see how the perfumer approached this idea.<br />
<br />
SHL accomplished his vision by having both in unison, with the top and mid of booze (without feeling like a liquor focused scent) and a heavier dose of cacao on a bed of vetiver, patchouli, vanilla and smooth woods. Typically, sand is represented with immortelle but it's possible that combination may have clashed. I personally would have chosen to include dates (fruit) and perhaps palm leaf to represent the desert, but this is his art, not mine.<br />
<br />
I'm picky about cacao but it's used well here and smells like good quality. A fun fragrance that I think will appeal to folks into artistic side of fragrances (me)and casual fans that just want something that smells good around their friends and family. However, I generally don't wear gourmand type scents very often so I'll probably sell it. Can be worn casual or formal, preferably in cool/cold temps. <br />
--------------------------------------------------------<br />
Overall a fun and well made fragrance. It doesn't smell like anything else in perfumery so points for originality. I'd say it's sort of the same vibe, but not the same smell as Kilian Black Phantom, if that makes sense. If you love the vibe of Phantom, you'll love this one. Strong performer, 3-4 sprays lasts me all night and has great sillage. <br />
<br />
🤎(°,,°)<br />
Scent 7.5/10<br />
Performance 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="2036280"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=2036280#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2019656" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; A dance steeped in tradition, seduction, with magical, hypnotic movements, enriched by veils, jewels and anklets, colourful: something extremely emotional, as Sand Dance is.<br />
A fragrance that opens spicy, projecting us into a different place, making us perceive that we will witness something extremely pleasant... the pure cocoa emerges,becoming inebriating thanks to the alcoholic notes and finally creamy and soft with the precious woods.<br />
An intense olfactory journey, a warm and decisive fragrance, which will not fail to please lovers of the genre.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="2019656"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=2019656#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1988342" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1188872">cdcs</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-25">09/25/23 18:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The whiskey is quite photorealistic to my nose. The first blast is sweet and smooth, and the sillage is great. Very good. But when the patchouli starts to creep up and mixes with the coriander and the warmth of the whiskey, up close to my skin I get the slightest hint of… pee? Probably a personal issue, though. Leans quite masculine for me, even though it has it’s fair share of sweetness. Unfortunately this didn’t come across vanillic enough to save it for me. Very pleasant, but not on me, not for me. Lasts long, strong patchouli, cacao and whiskey. Very ambery, but overall too much warmth for me and for the climate I live in.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1937311"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1937311#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1931318" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1931318" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="sorvaahr"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1642625"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1642625.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="sorvaahr" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Nicheend/Saturn-78217.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.78217.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Saturn"title="Saturn"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1931318ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1931318" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1642625">sorvaahr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-18">09/18/23 17:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>High time I give out a few words for this gem. Needless to say, I love it. My skin chemistry is incredibly acidic so florals often to complete messes (shame because I love them at times) but somehow, gourmands work wonders on me. A friend of mine was actually commenting earlier: "on anyone else I'd think this is annoying but you make it work somehow". <br />
<br />
Admittedly, and I've said it before, I'm not the alpha male type. Leather heavy, overly masculine chypres or fougeres are often wasted on me. Not that my skin messes them up, it's just that I don't look credible wearing them. So oftentimes, you'll find me wearing something either gourmands or incense/oud heavy Middle-Eastern fragrances. Sand Dance falls into the former, albeit with a tinge of a desert vibe, hence the name, referring to the infamous sidewinder snake it represents. Sand Dance opens with a beautiful blast of chocolate and whiskey before sweet vanillic benzoin shows up. The drydown on my skin is resinous and warm, powered by chocolatey patchouli and resinoids with creamy sandalwood rounding it up. Definitely a fall/winter scent, ideally on nights out. The longevity is fantastic, well over 8-10 hours on me, with the first 3-4 hours pushing out quite a bit within arms length. <br />
<br />
It is a beast of its own, but those who like Killian's Black Phantom might find much to enjoy here, not so much in the similarity of the scent but rather, in the general vibe, seasons and situations they're suitable in.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1362658">Divinest</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-11-22">11/22/22 00:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My thoughts upon initial spray, without looking at accords or pyramid: Definitely smelled this before. Sweet, amber fragrance. Slightly boozy in the opening. Mildly reminds me of Black Phantom as it dries. And Black Phantom is starting to overpower in the air. And then it kind-of goes away again. But I still think it's a derivative/play on Black Phantom. More ambery in the open, and I think it's more woody than it is gourmand in the drydown.<br />
<br />
After pyramid and accords: woody, warm spicy, amber, cacao. I was getting chocolatey facets, but wasn't 100% sure of it. I think it's fair to say this dries as chocolatey wood. Warm spices effectively fade off the top within 10 minutes, and you are left with sweetened woods. In the drydown, the best comparison to this profile is Xerjoff's Amber Star. That whiskey accord that I see other commenters referring to - it actually isn't strong enough to the point where I'd say whiskey is a prominent accord, just like how the rum in Black Phantom isn't a prominent accord.<br />
<br />
Longevity around 10 hours, sillage was strong for a couple hours (but will be moderate mostly), value on this entire house is meh - if you love something, buy it; otherwise you can get better value elsewhere. Profile... either unisex or slightly leaning masculine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1693538"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1693538#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1684078" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1666811" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="jassca99"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/614231"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.614231.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="jassca99" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1666811ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1666811" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/614231">jassca99</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-10-15">10/15/22 13:08</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The blast at first is too much liquor and you’ll need to wait a little before going in for a whiff. Then chocolate and whiskey! With an aromatic, kitchen spice underlay (the kind predominant in Xerjoff Ivory Route). I don’t want to say cacao because it’s not as dry and powdered. I also don’t get mandarin but the chocolate is probably not as dense because it’s there somewhere. Then the whiskey dies down and the chocolate remains and there’s a resinous feel, a little like myrrh, with a slightly pickled but smooth sandalwood. That lasts for the next hour with the best parts of tonka bean checking in later on; maybe because the other woody and resinous notes help prevent the tonka from getting too powdery, drawing out its nutty sweetness. In the dry down, which comes quick after 1-2 hours, the chocolate leaves and I’m left with myrrh, lots of creamy sandalwood and tonka. It stays like this for the rest of the wear. This is more interesting in the beginning, but it’s still beautiful and sweet enough afterwards. Not something I would see myself using up but it’s well made. Also radiates far on my skin in the beginning but closes in with time.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1666811"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1666811#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1639156" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; So yeah if you're actually a fan of that note in fragrances this is an obvious must try. The opening needs a little time to settle but once it does its a superb blend of whiskey and cacao and it gives it this sort of semi-gourmand feel and after some time the vanilla shows up giving it a smooth almost creamy vibe underneath the whiskey.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is very sexy and honestly deserves a lot more attention from the community. I could see this being a compliment-beast in colder weather. Love it. Edit since owning a full bottle: This is indeed a compliment beast, it has excellent projection and longevity.. the bottle also opens smoothly whereas my sample didn't in the opening so this makes it even more lovely to my nose.<br />
<br />
Would I buy: Own a full bottle<br />
Recommended: Absolutely, here before the hype train - but if it doesn't get hyped its an hidden gem.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1570076"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1570076#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                    </div>

The sandalwood is a little dustier, and the milk is more caramelized. It resembles toffee or dulce de leche whereas JDP is more of a saccharine milk. This dries down into suave santal. Beautifully done.<br />
<br />
I give this a thumbs up; however, it is not particularly original. I’m still waiting for more of the SHL that blew me away: Black Gemstone, Mortal Skin, Wish Come True, Generation 2022, O Hira.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1603348"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1603348#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1693538" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Sweet, amber fragrance. Slightly boozy in the opening. Mildly reminds me of Black Phantom as it dries. And Black Phantom is starting to overpower in the air. And then it kind-of goes away again. But I still think it's a derivative/play on Black Phantom. More ambery in the open, and I think it's more woody than it is gourmand in the drydown.<br />
<br />
After pyramid and accords: woody, warm spicy, amber, cacao. I was getting chocolatey facets, but wasn't 100% sure of it. I think it's fair to say this dries as chocolatey wood. Warm spices effectively fade off the top within 10 minutes, and you are left with sweetened woods. In the drydown, the best comparison to this profile is Xerjoff's Amber Star. That whiskey accord that I see other commenters referring to - it actually isn't strong enough to the point where I'd say whiskey is a prominent accord, just like how the rum in Black Phantom isn't a prominent accord.<br />
<br />
Longevity around 10 hours, sillage was strong for a couple hours (but will be moderate mostly), value on this entire house is meh - if you love something, buy it; otherwise you can get better value elsewhere. Profile... either unisex or slightly leaning masculine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1693538"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1693538#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1678227" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1642625">sorvaahr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-18">09/18/23 17:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>High time I give out a few words for this gem. Needless to say, I love it. My skin chemistry is incredibly acidic so florals often to complete messes (shame because I love them at times) but somehow, gourmands work wonders on me. A friend of mine was actually commenting earlier: "on anyone else I'd think this is annoying but you make it work somehow". <br />
<br />
Admittedly, and I've said it before, I'm not the alpha male type. Leather heavy, overly masculine chypres or fougeres are often wasted on me. Not that my skin messes them up, it's just that I don't look credible wearing them. So oftentimes, you'll find me wearing something either gourmands or incense/oud heavy Middle-Eastern fragrances. Sand Dance falls into the former, albeit with a tinge of a desert vibe, hence the name, referring to the infamous sidewinder snake it represents. Sand Dance opens with a beautiful blast of chocolate and whiskey before sweet vanillic benzoin shows up. The drydown on my skin is resinous and warm, powered by chocolatey patchouli and resinoids with creamy sandalwood rounding it up. Definitely a fall/winter scent, ideally on nights out. The longevity is fantastic, well over 8-10 hours on me, with the first 3-4 hours pushing out quite a bit within arms length. <br />
<br />
It is a beast of its own, but those who like Killian's Black Phantom might find much to enjoy here, not so much in the similarity of the scent but rather, in the general vibe, seasons and situations they're suitable in.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1931318"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1931318#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="72384" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1625142" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="rbalkris"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1068449"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1068449.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="rbalkris" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tiziana-Terenzi/Wezen-88305.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.88305.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Wezen"title="Wezen"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1625142ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1625142" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1068449">rbalkris</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-08-16">08/16/22 19:21</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Pleasant but cliched woody gourmand scent that displays none of the flair this perfumer is known for. The scent opens with notes of coriander, orange and whiskey. The heart is cacao, cashmeran and sandalwood. The perfume settles very fast into a powdery bed of patchouli, cedar, benzoin, and styrax. The sweet unisex scent has moderate to strong projection and good longevity. Really a ‘been there done that’ scent, but cheery and inoffensive. Enjoy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1625142"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1625142#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1937311" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1937311" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="cdcs"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1188872"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="cdcs" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Initio-Parfums-Prives/Narcotic-Delight-89368.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.89368.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Narcotic Delight"title="Narcotic Delight"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1937311ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1937311" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1188872">cdcs</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-25">09/25/23 18:40</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The whiskey is quite photorealistic to my nose. The first blast is sweet and smooth, and the sillage is great. Very good. But when the patchouli starts to creep up and mixes with the coriander and the warmth of the whiskey, up close to my skin I get the slightest hint of… pee? Probably a personal issue, though. Leans quite masculine for me, even though it has it’s fair share of sweetness. Unfortunately this didn’t come across vanillic enough to save it for me. Very pleasant, but not on me, not for me. Lasts long, strong patchouli, cacao and whiskey. Very ambery, but overall too much warmth for me and for the climate I live in.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="72384"comment_id="1937311"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Stephane-Humbert-Lucas-777/Sand-Dance-72384.html?ccid=1937311#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1590709" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
